### Game Theory

- `P1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: root fixation / completion / formative principle line.
  Confidence: mixed

## Direct Operational Meaning

`f86v6` behaves as `global integrator` inside the nine-rosette network.

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f86v6` is a routed network panel rather than a local recipe leaf.

## Mythic Extraction

Across the mythic lenses, `f86v6` is a district in the manuscript's hidden city.

## All-Lens Zero Point

`synchronize the whole rosette network and close it under one terminal law`

## Dense One-Sentence Compression

`f86v6` = synchronize the whole rosette network and close it under one terminal law.

\[\mathcal H := L^2(\widehat{\mathbb C}, \mu), \qquad \rho \in \mathcal T_1(\mathcal H), \qquad \rho \succeq 0, \qquad \mathrm{Tr}(\rho)=1\]

\[\mathcal H_{\mathrm{tot}} = \left(\bigoplus_r \mathcal H_r\right) \oplus \left(\bigoplus_e \mathcal H_{\Lambda_e}\right) \oplus \mathcal H_{\mathrm{fail}}\]

\[g = \mathrm{Coll}(X), \qquad X = \mathrm{Expand}(g) \oplus r\]

\[\Phi_j^{(\lambda)} = T_\lambda^{-1} \circ \Phi_j^{(\mathrm{AQM})} \circ T_\lambda\]

### Folio Theorem

\[\rho_* = (\Psi_{\mathrm{terminal}} \circ \Psi_{\mathrm{body}} \circ \Psi_{\mathrm{entry}})(\rho_0)\]

4. it contributes `global integrator` to the Book IV crystal
